<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀποθέωσις</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apothéōsis</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апофеоз.html>апофео́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">apofeóz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апофеоз.html>апофео́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апофеоз.html>апофео́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апофеоз.html>апофео́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apotheosis <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a glorified example or ideal; the apex or pinnacle (of a concept or belief)</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***аппарат.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппарат</a> (1493)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">apparātus</i>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Apparat</i>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">apparatus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́т</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">apparát</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́та</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́тов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>apparatus, instrument, device</li>
<li>camera</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">politics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> apparat, State organ, the machinery of state bureaucratic administration
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государственный.html>госуда́рственный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Gosudárstvennyj <b>apparát</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">State apparat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:военный.html>вое́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vojénnyj <b>apparát</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">military apparat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:партийный.html>парти́йный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:аппарат.html>аппара́т</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Partíjnyj <b>apparát</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">party apparat</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аппетит.html>аппети́т</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">appetít</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***апрель.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апрель</a> (3132)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">апрѣль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aprělĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, earlier <span class="Cyrs" lang="orv">априль</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="tr Latn">aprilĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Απρίλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aprílios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Aprīlis</i> from (perhaps) Etruscan <i class="Ital mention" lang="ett">𐌀𐌐𐌓𐌖</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ett-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">apru</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ἀφροδίτη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aphrodítē</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The form with <i>ѣ</i> in the second syllable is explained by Sobolevsky as a loan from the Novgorodian written language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aprélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>April
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ле</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>apréle</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in April</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>apréle</b> étovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in April</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прошлый.html>про́шлого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>apréle</b> próšlovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">April of last year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ле</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:будущее.html>бу́дущего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>apréle</b> búduščevo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">April of next year</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ля</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">do <b>aprélja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">until April</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́ля</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:декабрь.html>дека́брь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>aprélja</b> po dekábrʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from April to December</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:апрель.html>апре́лю</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>aprélju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by April</span></div></dd>

***аптекарь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарь.html>апте́карь</a> (9646)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптека.html>апте́ка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aptéka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-арь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-arʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарь.html>апте́карь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aptékarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарь.html>апте́каря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарь.html>апте́кари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарь.html>апте́карей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">апте́карша</b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптекарский.html>апте́карский</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pharmacist, chemist, druggist (male or female)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Grammatically the word is a masculine, but it is used to refer to both a man and a woman and it is declinable in both cases. The term <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">апте́карша</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aptékarša</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is also used for a woman in colloquial Russian.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аптека.html>апте́ка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">aptéka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:арабский.html>ара́бский</a> (7288)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:араб.html>ара́б</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aráb</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арабский.html>ара́бский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arábskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>Arabic, Arabian</li>
<li>Arab

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́п</a> (16412)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">арапъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arapŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr">Arap</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Arab</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́п</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aráp</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́па</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́пы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арап.html>ара́пов</a></b>)

***арба.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арба́</a> (18448)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">عَرَبَة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʿaraba</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">vehicle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арба́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arbá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арбы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>а́рбы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арб</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>araba (a horse- or bullock-drawn cart with two large wheels)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1829</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alexander_Pushkin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alexander Pushkin">Alexander Pushkin</a>,  <cite>Тазит</cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шествие.html>ше́ствие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:готовый.html>гото́во</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>И</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тронуться.html>тро́нулась</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арба́</a></b>. <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ней</a> / Адехи <a href = vnd.unilang:следовать.html>сле́дуют</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́во</a>, / <a href = vnd.unilang:смирять.html>смиря́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пыл.html>пыл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:конь.html>коне́й</a>...</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V dorógu šéstvije gotóvo, / I trónulasʹ <b>arbá</b>. Za nej / Adexi slédujut suróvo, / Smirjája molča pyl konéj...</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">On the road the procession is ready and the <b>cart</b> has set off. The Adyge men follow grimly after it, silently subduing the ardor of the horses...</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1891</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%94%D1%83%D1%8D%D0%BB%D1%8C_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)VI" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Дуэль (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:дуэль.html>Дуэ́ль</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Novoye_Vremya_(newspaper)" class="extiw" title="w:Novoye Vremya (newspaper)"><a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>Но́вое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></a></cite> |  republished as  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Duel_(Chekhov/Garnett)/Chapter_6" class="extiw" title="s:The Duel (Chekhov/Garnett)/Chapter 6">The Duel</a>”, in Larissa Volokhonsky; Richard Pevear, transl., <cite>The Complete Short Novels</cite>, 2004:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Пррава! — <a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рло</a> само́йленко, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:попадаться.html>попада́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:навстречу.html>навстре́чу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:арба.html>арба́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>и́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:абхазец.html>абха́зец</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верхо́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> осле́.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Prrava! — kričál vo vsjó górlo Samójlenko, kogdá popadálasʹ navstréču <b>arbá</b> íli abxázec verxóm na oslé.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Keep r-r-right!" ***арбитр.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:арбитр.html>арби́тр</a> (18814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арбитр.html>арби́тр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arbítr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арбитр.html>арби́тра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арбитр.html>арби́тры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арбитр.html>арби́тров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> arbiter, arbitrator (to resolve controversy)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> referee, umpire</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">арбузъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arbuzŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خربز</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xarbuz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">argumént</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нтов</a></b>)

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arrenda</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">reddo</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендатор.html>аренда́тор</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arendátor</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендатор.html>аренда́тора</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендатор.html>аренда́торы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендатор.html>аренда́торов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tenant (one who pays a fee in return for the use of land, etc.)</li></ol>

***арендовать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:арендовать.html>арендова́ть</a> (14764)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">arendować</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">arenda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arrenda</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">arrendare</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*adrendare</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">reddere</i>; see there for more.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендовать.html>арендова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">arendovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to lease; to rent</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арендатор.html>аренда́тор</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">arendátor</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">арендова́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">arendovánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:арестант.html>ареста́нт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arestánt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
